 The Kings XI Punjab team on Thursday scored 67th of the sixth edition of the Indian Premier League (IPL) played at the Himachal Pradesh Cricket Association (HPCA) ground on Thursday, thanks to the brilliant performance of their batsmen and bowlers, led by stormy innings David Miller
 They have kept their hopes of reaching their playoffs by beating Delhi Daredevils by seven runs in the 15th match
 iske liye haalanki use samikarnon ke apane haq main aane kaa intjaar karnaa hoga
 This is Delhi's 12th defeat in 15 matches
 toss harkar pehle ballebaaji karne utari kings ilevan punjab ne dilli dairedevills ke saamne jeet ke liye 172 ranon kaa lakshya rakhaa tha lekin dilli kii team lakshya kaa peechha karte hue lay se bhatak gai or 20 overon main saat wicket par 164 ran hi bana saki
 For Punjab, Sandeep Sharma took three wickets while Piyush Chawla got two successes
 miller ko main of da match chunaa gaya
 Kings XI have 12 points after this win
 uskaa plaof main pahunchnaa ab royal chalangers bangalore or sunrisers hyderabad kii haar par nirbhar karata he
 However, to qualify for the final-4 of Kings XI, they will have to win their last league match against Mumbai Indians
 vaise kings ilevan ke liye chintaa kii baat yah he ki sunrisers ke khate main do match bache hai
 Delhi started badly
 captain mahela jayavardhane (39) ke saath pari kii shuruyaat karne aae unmukt chand (7) ko 11 ran ke kul yoga par praveen kumaar ne chalata kiya
 After this, Irfan Pathan (1) and David Warner (0) kept going on the total of 12 runs
 pathan or warner ko sandip sharma ne out kiya
 After this, Virender Sehwag (30) raised hopes for the fourth wicket with the skipper adding 49 runs from 39 balls but Sehwag's poor form did not stop him and he was dismissed by Parvinder Awana for a total of 61 runs
 sahvaag ne 22 gedon kii pari main chah chauke lagaae
 After Sehwag's dismissal, Jayawardene added 50 for the fifth wicket with Ben Rohrer (49)
 in donon ne ye ran 33 gendon par banaae
 The fast-paced partnership was broken by Sandeep at a grand total of 111
 sandip ne 42 gendon par teen chauke or ek chakka lagane vaale jayavardhane ko manan vohara ke haathon kaich karaayaa
 Rohrer played a brilliant innings and was dismissed when Delhi needed 22 runs off 6 balls
 vah wicket par rahete to is lakshya ko hasil kiya ja saktaa tha
 Rohrer hit four fours and three sixes off 29 balls
 unhone muralidharan gautam (naabad 12) ke saath chathe wicket ke liye 18 gendon par 39 ran jode
 After Rohrer's dismissal, Morne Morkel (13) added 14 runs in Chawla's over but Morkel was dismissed on the final ball
 morkal ne chaar gendon par do chakke lagaae
 Earlier, Captain Adam Gilchrist, who helped Kings XI win against Royal Challengers in the previous match, gave his team a decent start in this match
 salaami ballebaajon ke behtareen pradarshan ke alaava aakhri over main tej banaae gaye ranon kii badaulat kings ilevan ne nirdhaarit 20 overon main chaar wicket par 171 ranon kaa score khadaa kiya
 Gilchrist (42) and Shaun Marsh (45) shared a 60-run partnership for the first wicket
 gilcrist aathven over kii teesri gend par irfan pathan ke haathon cott and bold hue
 Gilchrist hit five fours and two sixes in 26 balls
 pichley match main royal chalangers ke khilaaf jeet dilaane main gilcrist ke saath mahatvapurn pari khilne vaale ajahar mahmud (9) haalanki kuch khaas nahin kar sake or kings ilevan ke yoga main 26 ran jodakar siddharth kaul ke haathon kaich out hue
 Opener Marsh also performed well
 unhone 44 gendon kaa saamana kar saat chauke lagaae
 Marsh Morkel got caught by Pathan at the hands of Pathan
 tippaniyan After this, David Miller (44) and Rajagopal Satish (22) added 47 runs in the last 18 balls for Kings XI in the fourth wicket partnership to raise Kings XI score to 171
 miller ne kaaphi aakraamak tareeke se khelte hue 24 gendon main teen chauke tathaa chaar chakke lagaae
 Satish was caught by Ben Rohrer on the fifth ball of the last over
 dairedevills ke liye ashish nehra no do wicket tathaa pathan or morkal ne ek-ek wicket liya
 Batting first after losing the toss, Kings XI Punjab had set a target of 172 runs for victory in front of Delhi Daredevils but the Delhi team deviated from the chasing target and managed 164 runs for seven wickets in 20 overs
 punjab kii ore se sandip sharma ne teen wicket liye jabaki piyush chawla ko do safalataa mili
 Miller was voted man of the match
 is jeet ke baad kings ilevan ke 12 ank ho gaye hai
 His reach in the playoffs now depends on the defeat of Royal Challengers Bangalore and Sunrisers Hyderabad
 vaise kings ilevan ke antim-4 ke liye kwalifai karne ke liye mumbai indiens ke khilaaf apana antim lig match har haal main jeetna hoga
 However, what is worrying for Kings XI is that Sunrisers have two matches left in their account
 dilli kii shuruyaat kharaab rahi
 Unmukt Chand (7), who started the innings with captain Mahela Jayawardene (39), was run by Praveen Kumar for a total of 11 runs
 iske baad 12 ran ke kul yoga par irfan pathan (1) or isi yoga par david warner (0) chalate bane
 Pathan and Warner were dismissed by Sandeep Sharma
 iske baad virendra sahvaag (30) ne captain ke saath chauthe wicket ke liye 39 gendon par 49 ran jodakar ummid jagaai lekin sahvaag ke kharaab farm ne unka saath nahin choda or vah 61 ranon ke kul yoga par parvinder awana kii gend par out ho gaye
 Sehwag hit six fours in 22 balls
 sahvaag ke out hone ke baad jayavardhane ne ben rohrer (49) ke saath paanchaven wicket ke liye 50 ran jode
 Both of them scored these runs off 33 balls
 teji se jari is saajhedaari ko sandip ne 111 ke kul yoga par todaa
 Sandeep had Jayawardene caught by Manan Vohra, who hit three fours and a six off 42 balls
 rohrer ne ek shandaar pari kheli or us samay out hue jab dilli ko 6 gendon par 22 ranon kii jarurat thi
 Had he been on the wicket, this goal could have been achieved
 rohrer ne 29 gendon par chaar chauke or teen chakke lagaae
 He added 39 runs from 18 balls for the sixth wicket with Muralitharan Gautam (12 not out)
 rohrer ke out hone ke baad morne morkal (13) ne chawla ke over main 14 ran batore lekin antim gend par morkal out ho gaye
 Morkel hit two sixes off four balls
 isse pehle, pichley match main kings ilevan ko royal chalangers ke khilaaf jeet dilaane vaale captain adam gilcrist ne is match main bhi apni team ko sadhi hui shuruyaat di
 Apart from the best performance of the openers, thanks to the runs scored in the last over, Kings XI scored 171 runs for four wickets in the prescribed 20 overs
 gilcrist (42) tathaa shaun marsh (45) ke bich pehle wicket ke liye 60 ranon kii saajhedaari hui
 Gilchrist was caught and bowled by Irfan Pathan on the third ball of the eighth over
 gilcrist ne 26 gendon main paanch chauke tathaa do chakke lagaae
 Azhar Mahmood (9), who played a crucial innings with Gilchrist in helping them win against Royal Challengers in the previous match, however could not do much and Siddharth Kaul was caught out by adding 26 runs to the total of Kings XI
 salaami ballebaaj marsh ne bhi behtareen pradarshan kiya
 He hit seven fours facing 44 balls
 marsh ko morne morkel ne pathan ke haathon kaich out karaayaa
 The comments iske baad chauthe wicket kii saajhedaari main david miller (44) tathaa rajagopal satish (22) ne kings ilevan ke liye aakhri 18 gendon main 47 ran jodakar kings ilevan kaa score 171 tak pahunchaa diya
 Miller played very aggressively, hitting three fours and four sixes in 24 balls
 aakhri over kii paanchavin gend par satish ko ben rohrer ne lapak liya
 For the Daredevils, Ashish Nehra took two wickets and Pathan and Morkel took one wicket each

 haalanki agar ve in donon muddon raji hai to aaj raat tak jawaab de den, baatcheet kal se hi shuru ho jaaegi or iskaa nateeja jarur nikalegaa
